## Instruction

Please read the table titled "GDP2022" in Google Sheets and calculate the CR5 index for each of the seven major regions listed by the World Bank. Create a new spreadsheet in Google Sheets, name it "GDP CR5 Analysis", and within it, create a new table titled "gdp_cr5_analysis". Save the following data with headers being `Region`, `Top5_Countries`, `Top5_GDP_Sum`, `Region_GDP_Total`, and `CR5_Ratio`, where they represent the region name, the top five countries (use exactly the full names in existing sheet and separated by "/", from highest to lowest), the sum of the top five countries' GDP, the total regional GDP, and the CR5 index (percentage, rounded to two decimal places). Sort the data in descending order by CR5 index. 

Note: You should strictly following the country classification provided by the World Bank. If one region has less than 5 countries, you just consider the real number of countries in filling the table.

## Initial State

### Google Sheets

The Google Sheet is reinitialized on each test; you can view the original data [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/gdp-cr5-analysis/preprocess).

```python
# Let me get a simpler view of the data structure first
import json

# I need to read the complete data from the saved file to understand the structure
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/RPeBo5Lu4QT8iGBiWaPSFn.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

# Extract just the basic structure to understand columns and first few rows
sheets = data['sheets']
country_sheet = sheets[0]  # First sheet is "Country"
row_data = country_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

# Get headers from first row
headers = []
for cell in row_data[0]['values']:
    if 'userEnteredValue' in cell:
        headers.append(cell['userEnteredValue'].get('stringValue', ''))
    elif 'effectiveValue' in cell:
        headers.append(cell['effectiveValue'].get('stringValue', ''))

print("Headers:", headers)

# Get first few data rows
print("\nFirst 5 data rows:")
for i in range(1, min(6, len(row_data))):
    row = []
    for cell in row_data[i]['values']:
        if 'userEnteredValue' in cell:
            if 'stringValue' in cell['userEnteredValue']:
                row.append(cell['userEnteredValue']['stringValue'])
            elif 'numberValue' in cell['userEnteredValue']:
                row.append(cell['userEnteredValue']['numberValue'])
        elif 'effectiveValue' in cell:
            if 'stringValue' in cell['effectiveValue']:
                row.append(cell['effectiveValue']['stringValue'])
            elif 'numberValue' in cell['effectiveValue']:
                row.append(cell['effectiveValue']['numberValue'])
    print(f"Row {i}: {row}") code
```

```python
import json

# Read the saved data and check its structure
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/RPeBo5Lu4QT8iGBiWaPSFn.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

print("Top level keys:", list(data.keys()))
print("Type:", type(data))
if isinstance(data, dict):
    for key in data.keys():
        print(f"{key}: {type(data[key])}")
        if key == 'sheets' and isinstance(data[key], list):
            print(f"  Number of sheets: {len(data[key])}")
            for i, sheet in enumerate(data[key]):
                print(f"  Sheet {i}: {sheet.get('properties', {}).get('title', 'Unknown')}") code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import json

# Read the saved data and extract the actual JSON
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/RPeBo5Lu4QT8iGBiWaPSFn.json', 'r') as f:
    wrapper = json.load(f)

# Extract the actual JSON from the text field
actual_data = json.loads(wrapper['text'])

print("Top level keys:", list(actual_data.keys()))

# Get the sheets
sheets = actual_data['sheets']
print(f"Number of sheets: {len(sheets)}")

# Look at the Country sheet
country_sheet = sheets[0]
print(f"Country sheet title: {country_sheet['properties']['title']}")

# Get the row data
row_data = country_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']
print(f"Number of rows: {len(row_data)}")

# Get headers from first row
headers = []
for cell in row_data[0]['values']:
    if 'userEnteredValue' in cell:
        headers.append(cell['userEnteredValue'].get('stringValue', ''))
    elif 'effectiveValue' in cell:
        headers.append(cell['effectiveValue'].get('stringValue', ''))

print("Headers:", headers)

# Get first few data rows
print("\nFirst 5 data rows:")
for i in range(1, min(6, len(row_data))):
    row = []
    for cell in row_data[i]['values']:
        if 'userEnteredValue' in cell:
            if 'stringValue' in cell['userEnteredValue']:
                row.append(cell['userEnteredValue']['stringValue'])
            elif 'numberValue' in cell['userEnteredValue']:
                row.append(cell['userEnteredValue']['numberValue'])
        elif 'effectiveValue' in cell:
            if 'stringValue' in cell['effectiveValue']:
                row.append(cell['effectiveValue']['stringValue'])
            elif 'numberValue' in cell['effectiveValue']:
                row.append(cell['effectiveValue']['numberValue'])
    print(f"Row {i}: {row}") code
```

```python
import json
import pandas as pd

# First, I need to create a mapping between countries and their World Bank regions
# I'll need to get all the data from both sheets

# Load the Country sheet data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/RPeBo5Lu4QT8iGBiWaPSFn.json', 'r') as f:
    country_wrapper = json.load(f)
country_data = json.loads(country_wrapper['text'])

# Load the Region sheet data  
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/k2YcAXUESk462KyGMMkxDq.json', 'r') as f:
    region_wrapper = json.load(f)
region_data = json.loads(region_wrapper['text'])

# Extract country data
country_sheet = country_data['sheets'][0]
country_rows = country_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

countries = []
for i in range(1, len(country_rows)):  # Skip header
    row = country_rows[i]
    if len(row['values']) >= 4:
        country_code = row['values'][0].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        ranking = row['values'][1].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        country_name = row['values'][2].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        gdp = row['values'][3].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        
        if country_code and country_name and gdp > 0:
            countries.append({
                'code': country_code,
                'ranking': ranking,
                'name': country_name,
                'gdp': gdp
            })

print(f"Extracted {len(countries)} countries")

# Extract region data - I need to identify the 7 major World Bank regions
region_sheet = region_data['sheets'][0]
region_rows = region_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

regions = []
for i in range(1, len(region_rows)):  # Skip header
    row = region_rows[i]
    if len(row['values']) >= 3:
        region_code = row['values'][0].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        region_name = row['values'][1].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        region_gdp = row['values'][2].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        
        if region_code and region_name and region_gdp > 0:
            regions.append({
                'code': region_code,
                'name': region_name,
                'gdp': region_gdp
            })

print(f"Extracted {len(regions)} regions")
for region in regions:
    print(f"  {region['code']}: {region['name']} - GDP: {region['gdp']:,.0f}") code
```

`fetch fetch_json`

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import json
import pandas as pd

# Load the World Bank API country data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/fs8uPXvb2jjiG8fmCcGy7R.json', 'r') as f:
    wb_api_data = json.load(f)

wb_countries = json.loads(wb_api_data['text'])[1]  # Skip the metadata, get the actual data

# Create a mapping from country code to region
country_to_region = {}
for country in wb_countries:
    if country.get('region') and country['region']['id'] in ['EAS', 'ECS', 'LCN', 'MEA', 'NAC', 'SAS', 'SSF']:
        country_to_region[country['id']] = {
            'region_code': country['region']['id'],
            'region_name': country['region']['value']
        }

print(f"Found {len(country_to_region)} countries mapped to 7 major regions")

# Now load our GDP data and map countries to regions
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/RPeBo5Lu4QT8iGBiWaPSFn.json', 'r') as f:
    country_wrapper = json.load(f)
country_data = json.loads(country_wrapper['text'])

# Extract country data
country_sheet = country_data['sheets'][0]
country_rows = country_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

countries_with_regions = []
for i in range(1, len(country_rows)):  # Skip header
    row = country_rows[i]
    if len(row['values']) >= 4:
        country_code = row['values'][0].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        ranking = row['values'][1].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        country_name = row['values'][2].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        gdp = row['values'][3].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        
        if country_code and country_name and gdp > 0:
            # Map to region
            if country_code in country_to_region:
                countries_with_regions.append({
                    'code': country_code,
                    'ranking': ranking,
                    'name': country_name,
                    'gdp': gdp,
                    'region_code': country_to_region[country_code]['region_code'],
                    'region_name': country_to_region[country_code]['region_name']
                })

print(f"Successfully mapped {len(countries_with_regions)} countries to regions")

# Group by region and calculate CR5
regions_data = {}
for country in countries_with_regions:
    region_code = country['region_code']
    if region_code not in regions_data:
        regions_data[region_code] = {
            'region_name': country['region_name'],
            'countries': []
        }
    regions_data[region_code]['countries'].append(country)

print(f"Found data for {len(regions_data)} regions:")
for region_code, data in regions_data.items():
    print(f"  {region_code}: {data['region_name']} - {len(data['countries'])} countries") code
```

```python
# Calculate CR5 for each region
cr5_results = []

for region_code, data in regions_data.items():
    # Sort countries by GDP in descending order
    countries = sorted(data['countries'], key=lambda x: x['gdp'], reverse=True)
    
    # Calculate total regional GDP
    total_gdp = sum(country['gdp'] for country in countries)
    
    # Get top 5 countries (or all if less than 5)
    top_5 = countries[:5]
    top_5_gdp = sum(country['gdp'] for country in top_5)
    
    # Calculate CR5 ratio
    cr5_ratio = (top_5_gdp / total_gdp) * 100 if total_gdp > 0 else 0
    
    # Format top 5 country names
    top_5_names = [country['name'] for country in top_5]
    top_5_names_str = "/".join(top_5_names)
    
    cr5_results.append({
        'Region': data['region_name'].strip(),
        'Top5_Countries': top_5_names_str,
        'Top5_GDP_Sum': top_5_gdp,
        'Region_GDP_Total': total_gdp,
        'CR5_Ratio': round(cr5_ratio, 2)
    })
    
    print(f"\n{region_code}: {data['region_name']}")
    print(f"  Total countries: {len(countries)}")
    print(f"  Total GDP: ${total_gdp:,.0f} million")
    print(f"  Top 5 countries: {top_5_names_str}")
    print(f"  Top 5 GDP: ${top_5_gdp:,.0f} million")
    print(f"  CR5 ratio: {cr5_ratio:.2f}%")

# Sort by CR5 ratio in descending order
cr5_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['CR5_Ratio'], reverse=True)

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("FINAL CR5 RESULTS (sorted by CR5 ratio descending):")
print("="*80)
for i, result in enumerate(cr5_results, 1):
    print(f"{i}. {result['Region']}: {result['CR5_Ratio']}%")
    print(f"   Top 5: {result['Top5_Countries']}")
    print(f"   Top 5 GDP: ${result['Top5_GDP_Sum']:,.0f}M, Total GDP: ${result['Region_GDP_Total']:,.0f}M")
    print() code
```

```python
import json
import pandas as pd

# Load the World Bank API country data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/fs8uPXvb2jjiG8fmCcGy7R.json', 'r') as f:
    wb_api_data = json.load(f)

wb_countries = json.loads(wb_api_data['text'])[1]  # Skip the metadata, get the actual data

# Create a mapping from country code to region
country_to_region = {}
for country in wb_countries:
    if country.get('region') and country['region']['id'] in ['EAS', 'ECS', 'LCN', 'MEA', 'NAC', 'SAS', 'SSF']:
        country_to_region[country['id']] = {
            'region_code': country['region']['id'],
            'region_name': country['region']['value']
        }

# Load our GDP data and map countries to regions
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/RPeBo5Lu4QT8iGBiWaPSFn.json', 'r') as f:
    country_wrapper = json.load(f)
country_data = json.loads(country_wrapper['text'])

# Extract country data
country_sheet = country_data['sheets'][0]
country_rows = country_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

countries_with_regions = []
for i in range(1, len(country_rows)):  # Skip header
    row = country_rows[i]
    if len(row['values']) >= 4:
        country_code = row['values'][0].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        ranking = row['values'][1].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        country_name = row['values'][2].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        gdp = row['values'][3].get('userEnteredValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        
        if country_code and country_name and gdp > 0:
            # Map to region
            if country_code in country_to_region:
                countries_with_regions.append({
                    'code': country_code,
                    'ranking': ranking,
                    'name': country_name,
                    'gdp': gdp,
                    'region_code': country_to_region[country_code]['region_code'],
                    'region_name': country_to_region[country_code]['region_name']
                })

# Group by region
regions_data = {}
for country in countries_with_regions:
    region_code = country['region_code']
    if region_code not in regions_data:
        regions_data[region_code] = {
            'region_name': country['region_name'],
            'countries': []
        }
    regions_data[region_code]['countries'].append(country)

# Calculate CR5 for each region
cr5_results = []

for region_code, data in regions_data.items():
    # Sort countries by GDP in descending order
    countries = sorted(data['countries'], key=lambda x: x['gdp'], reverse=True)
    
    # Calculate total regional GDP
    total_gdp = sum(country['gdp'] for country in countries)
    
    # Get top 5 countries (or all if less than 5)
    top_5 = countries[:5]
    top_5_gdp = sum(country['gdp'] for country in top_5)
    
    # Calculate CR5 ratio
    cr5_ratio = (top_5_gdp / total_gdp) * 100 if total_gdp > 0 else 0
    
    # Format top 5 country names
    top_5_names = [country['name'] for country in top_5]
    top_5_names_str = "/".join(top_5_names)
    
    cr5_results.append({
        'Region': data['region_name'].strip(),
        'Top5_Countries': top_5_names_str,
        'Top5_GDP_Sum': top_5_gdp,
        'Region_GDP_Total': total_gdp,
        'CR5_Ratio': round(cr5_ratio, 2)
    })
    
    print(f"\n{region_code}: {data['region_name']}")
    print(f"  Total countries: {len(countries)}")
    print(f"  Total GDP: ${total_gdp:,.0f} million")
    print(f"  Top 5 countries: {top_5_names_str}")
    print(f"  Top 5 GDP: ${top_5_gdp:,.0f} million")
    print(f"  CR5 ratio: {cr5_ratio:.2f}%")

# Sort by CR5 ratio in descending order
cr5_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['CR5_Ratio'], reverse=True)

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("FINAL CR5 RESULTS (sorted by CR5 ratio descending):")
print("="*80)
for i, result in enumerate(cr5_results, 1):
    print(f"{i}. {result['Region']}: {result['CR5_Ratio']}%")
    print(f"   Top 5: {result['Top5_Countries']}")
    print(f"   Top 5 GDP: ${result['Top5_GDP_Sum']:,.0f}M, Total GDP: ${result['Region_GDP_Total']:,.0f}M")
    print()

# Store results for creating the spreadsheet
print("CR5 Results ready for spreadsheet creation:")
for result in cr5_results:
    print(result) code
```

```python
# Prepare the data for the spreadsheet

# Results already sorted by CR5 ratio descending

spreadsheet_data.append(headers)

# Add the sorted data
for result in cr5_results:
    row = [
        result['Region'],
        result['Top5_Countries'],
        result['Top5_GDP_Sum'],
        result['Region_GDP_Total'],
        result['CR5_Ratio']
    ]
    spreadsheet_data.append(row)
```

```python
print("RESULTS (sorted by CR5 ratio, descending):")
print("-" * 50)

results = [
    ("North America", "United States/Canada/Bermuda", 100.00),
    ("South Asia", "India/Bangladesh/Sri Lanka/Nepal/Maldives", 99.94),
    ("East Asia & Pacific", "China/Japan/Australia/Korea, Rep./Indonesia", 89.90),
    ("Latin America & Caribbean", "Brazil/Mexico/Argentina/Cuba/Colombia", 76.48),

    ("Sub-Saharan Africa", "Nigeria/South Africa/Ethiopia/Kenya/Angola", 60.33),
    ("Europe & Central Asia", "Germany/United Kingdom/France/Russian Federation/Italy", 56.31)
```
